<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities">Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/en-us/Nidalee?section=1&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Abilities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/en-us/Nidalee?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Abilities">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="skill skill_innate" style="padding: 1em; margin-top: 1em; box-shadow:black 0 2px 5px 0;color:#c8c4bd; border:#525244 solid 1px; background:#082848 no-repeat right top; overflow:hidden; position:relative; z-index: 100;">
<div id="Prowl" class="skill_header skill_wrapper"><span class="plainlinks"><a class="text" href="https://wiki.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/Template:Data_Nidalee/Prowl?action=edit"><span class="button" title="Click here to edit this ability." style="float:right; text-align:center; border-radius: 2px; position:absolute; right:13px; z-index:5"><b>&#160;Edit&#160;</b></span></a></span><div class="ability-info-container"><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_wrapper">
<div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_ability">Prowl</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_list"><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat"><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat-label">EFFECT RADIUS:</div><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat-value"><span class="basic-tooltip" style="border-bottom:1px dotted gray;cursor:help;" title="Hunt bonuses range">3000</span> / <span class="basic-tooltip" style="border-bottom:1px dotted gray;cursor:help;" title="Hunt increased bonus movement speed range">5500</span></div></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ability-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Innate - Prowl:</b></span> While in <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Brush"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Brush" title="Brush"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ivern_Brushmaker.png/20px-Ivern_Brushmaker.png?4c89b" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Ivern_Brushmaker.png/40px-Ivern_Brushmaker.png?4c89b 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Brush" title="Brush">brush</a></span>, <span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><span title="An icon representing Nidalee"><img alt="An icon representing Nidalee" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png?c6101" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png?c6101 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></span></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><strong class="selflink">Nidalee</strong></span></span> becomes <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Ghosted"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Unit_collision" title="Unit collision"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ghost.png/20px-Ghost.png?ee615" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Ghost.png/40px-Ghost.png?ee615 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Unit_collision" title="Unit collision">ghosted</a></span> and gains <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Movement_speed" title="Movement speed"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Movement_speed_icon.png/15px-Movement_speed_icon.png?f928e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Movement_speed_icon.png/30px-Movement_speed_icon.png?f928e 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<span style="color: #9FFF4D; white-space:normal"><b>bonus</b> movement speed</span></span> for a short time, increased when facing a nearby enemy <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Champion"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Champion" title="Champion"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Champion_icon.png/20px-Champion_icon.png?2d7b0" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Champion_icon.png/40px-Champion_icon.png?2d7b0 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Champion" title="Champion">champion</a></span>. These bonuses briefly persist after exiting brush. <span class="template_sbc"><b>Innate - Hunt:</b></span> Hitting nearby <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Monsters"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Monster" title="Monster"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Monster_icon.png/20px-Monster_icon.png?e9efe" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Monster_icon.png?e9efe 2x" data-file-width="24" data-file-height="24" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Monster" title="Monster">monsters</a></span> or enemy champions with <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Javelin Toss" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Javelin_Toss" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Javelin Toss"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Javelin Toss" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png/40px-Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png?9d69e 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Javelin_Toss">Javelin Toss</a></span></span></i> or <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Bushwhack" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Bushwhack" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Bushwhack"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Bushwhack" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Bushwhack.png/20px-Nidalee_Bushwhack.png?2263d" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Bushwhack">Bushwhack</a></span></span></i> will apply a <i>Hunted</i> mark and <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="True sight"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Sight#True_sight" title="Sight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/True_Sight_icon.png/20px-True_Sight_icon.png?8830f" decoding="async" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Sight#True_sight" title="Sight">reveal</a></span> them for a few seconds. During this time, <b>Nidalee</b> gains <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Movement_speed" title="Movement speed"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Movement_speed_icon.png/15px-Movement_speed_icon.png?f928e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Movement_speed_icon.png/30px-Movement_speed_icon.png?f928e 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<span style="color: #9FFF4D; white-space:normal"><b>bonus</b> movement speed</span></span>, increased when facing a <i>Hunted</i> target. <b>Nidalee's</b> first use of <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Takedown" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Takedown" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/20px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/40px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Takedown">Takedown</a></span></span></i> and <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Pounce" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Pounce" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Pounce"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Pounce" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Pounce.png/20px-Nidalee_Pounce.png?b56c7" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Pounce.png/40px-Nidalee_Pounce.png?b56c7 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Pounce">Pounce</a></span></span></i> against <i>Hunted</i> targets are empowered. </div><div class="ability-info-content"><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span></div>
<div class="ability-info-description no-stats"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Innate - Prowl:</b></span> While in <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Brush"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Brush" title="Brush"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ivern_Brushmaker.png/20px-Ivern_Brushmaker.png?4c89b" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Ivern_Brushmaker.png/40px-Ivern_Brushmaker.png?4c89b 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Brush" title="Brush">brush</a></span>, <b>Nidalee</b> gains <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Ghosting"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Unit_collision" title="Unit collision"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ghost.png/20px-Ghost.png?ee615" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Ghost.png/40px-Ghost.png?ee615 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Unit_collision" title="Unit collision">ghosting</a></span> and <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Movement_speed" title="Movement speed"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Movement_speed_icon.png/15px-Movement_speed_icon.png?f928e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Movement_speed_icon.png/30px-Movement_speed_icon.png?f928e 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<span style="color: #9FFF4D; white-space:normal">10% <b>bonus</b> movement speed</span></span>, increased to <span style="color: #9FFF4D; white-space:normal">30%</span> while facing a <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Sight"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Sight" title="Sight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Sight_icon.png/20px-Sight_icon.png?0aaf0" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Sight_icon.png?0aaf0 2x" data-file-width="26" data-file-height="26" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Sight" title="Sight">visible</a></span> enemy <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Champion"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Champion" title="Champion"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Champion_icon.png/20px-Champion_icon.png?2d7b0" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Champion_icon.png/40px-Champion_icon.png?2d7b0 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Champion" title="Champion">champion</a></span> within 1400 range. The bonuses persist for 2 seconds after leaving brush.</div>

<div class="ability-info-icon"></div>
<div class="ability-info-description no-stats"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Innate - Hunt:</b></span> Hitting <a href="/en-us/Monsters" class="mw-redirect" title="Monsters">monsters</a> or enemy <a href="/en-us/Champions" class="mw-redirect" title="Champions">champions</a> with <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Javelin Toss" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Javelin_Toss" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Javelin Toss"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Javelin Toss" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png/20px-Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png?9d69e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png/40px-Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png?9d69e 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Javelin_Toss">Javelin Toss</a></span></span></i> or <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Bushwhack" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Bushwhack" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Bushwhack"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Bushwhack" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Bushwhack.png/20px-Nidalee_Bushwhack.png?2263d" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Bushwhack.png/40px-Nidalee_Bushwhack.png?2263d 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Bushwhack">Bushwhack</a></span></span></i> when <b>Nidalee</b> is nearby grants her <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Ghosting"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Unit_collision" title="Unit collision"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ghost.png/20px-Ghost.png?ee615" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Ghost.png/40px-Ghost.png?ee615 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Unit_collision" title="Unit collision">ghosting</a></span> and <span style="color: #9FFF4D; white-space:normal">10% <b>bonus</b> movement speed</span> for 4 seconds and applies a <i>Hunted</i> mark to the target for the same duration, during which they are <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="True sight"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Sight#True_sight" title="Sight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/True_Sight_icon.png/20px-True_Sight_icon.png?8830f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/True_Sight_icon.png/40px-True_Sight_icon.png?8830f 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Sight#True_sight" title="Sight">revealed</a></span> as well as grant <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Sight"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Sight" title="Sight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Sight_icon.png/20px-Sight_icon.png?0aaf0" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Sight_icon.png?0aaf0 2x" data-file-width="26" data-file-height="26" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Sight" title="Sight">sight</a></span> of a 300-unit radius around them. The <span style="color: #9FFF4D; white-space:normal"><b>bonus</b> movement speed</span> is increased to <span style="color: #9FFF4D; white-space:normal">30%</span> while facing a <i>Hunted</i> target. Additionally, the first cast of both <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Takedown" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Takedown" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/20px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/40px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Takedown">Takedown</a></span></span></i> and <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Pounce" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Pounce" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Pounce"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Pounce" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Pounce.png/20px-Nidalee_Pounce.png?b56c7" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Pounce.png/40px-Nidalee_Pounce.png?b56c7 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Pounce">Pounce</a></span></span></i> against a <i>Hunted</i> target is enhanced.</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats"></div>
</div><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"></div>
<div class="ability-info-description no-stats">The <span style="color: #9FFF4D; white-space:normal"><b>bonus</b> movement speed</span> from <i>Prowl</i> and <i>Hunt</i> can stack, but cannot exceed <span style="color: #9FFF4D; white-space:normal">30%</span>.</div>

<div class="ability-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Active:</b></span> <span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><span title="An icon representing Nidalee"><img alt="An icon representing Nidalee" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png?c6101" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png?c6101 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></span></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><strong class="selflink">Nidalee</strong></span></span> hurls a javelin in the target direction that deals <span style="color: #00B0F0; white-space:normal">magic damage</span> to the first enemy hit based on distance travelled.   </div><div class="ability-info-content"><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png?9d69e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span></div>
<div class="ability-info-description"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Active:</b></span> <b>Nidalee</b> hurls a javelin in the target direction that deals <span style="color: #00B0F0; white-space:normal">magic damage</span> to the first enemy hit, increased by <span class="pp-tooltip" style="position:relative; border-bottom:1px dotted; cursor:help;" data-top_label="distance traveled" data-start="0;525" data-finish="225;1300" data-bot_values="0;45;90;135;180;225" data-top_values="525;680;835;990;1145;1300" data-bot_key="%">0% – 225% (based on distance traveled)</span>.</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats"><dl class="skill-tabs" style="letter-spacing:0.02rem;"><dt><span class="template_lc"><b>Minimum Magic Damage:</b></span></dt><dd>70 / 90 / 110 / 130 / 150 <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">(+ 50% AP)</span></dd><dt><span class="template_lc"><b>Maximum Magic Damage:</b></span></dt><dd>227.<small>5</small> / 292.<small>5</small> / 357.<small>5</small> / 422.<small>5</small> / 487.<small>5</small> <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">(+ 162.<small>5</small>% AP)</span></dd></dl></div>
</div></div><div class="ability-info-flavor"></div></div></div></div>

</p><div style="display:none;"><b>Info</b><br /></div>
<div style="padding:0.5em 1em;"><div class="infobox"><div class="infobox-section-stacked"><div class="infobox-data-row"><div class="infobox-data-label">Targeting input</div><div class="infobox-data-value"><a href="/en-us/Targeting#Direction" title="Targeting">Direction</a></div></div></div><div class="infobox-header">Damage classification</div><div class="infobox-section-cell"><div class="infobox-data-row"><div class="infobox-data-label">Type</div><div class="infobox-data-value"><span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Spell damage"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Damage" title="Damage"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Annie_Disintegrate.png/56px-Annie_Disintegrate.png?bbde6" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="56" height="56" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Annie_Disintegrate.png?bbde6 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span><br /><a href="/en-us/Damage" title="Damage">Spell damage</a></span></div></div><div class="infobox-data-row"><div class="infobox-data-label">Sub-type(s)</div><div class="infobox-data-value"><span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Magic damage"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Magic_damage" title="Magic damage"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Magic_damage.png/56px-Magic_damage.png?2db19" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="56" height="56" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Magic_damage.png/112px-Magic_damage.png?2db19 2x" data-file-width="163" data-file-height="163" /></a></span><br /><a href="/en-us/Magic_damage" title="Magic damage">Magic</a></span></div></div></div><div class="infobox-header">Counters</div><div class="infobox-section-cell"><div class="infobox-data-row"><div class="infobox-data-label">Spell shield</div><div class="infobox-data-value"><span title="This ability will be blocked by spell shields. • Edge of Night • Banshee&#39;s Veil • Nocturne&#39;s Shroud of Darkness • Sivir&#39;s Spell Shield"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Sivir_Spell_Shield.png/56px-Sivir_Spell_Shield.png?4c4d1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="56" height="56" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Sivir_Spell_Shield.png?4c4d1 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span><br />Blocked</span></div></div><div class="infobox-data-row"><div class="infobox-data-label">Projectile</div><div class="infobox-data-value"><span title="This ability will be intercepted by Yasuo&#39;s Wind Wall, Braum&#39;s Unbreakable, Samira&#39;s Blade Whirl, and Mel&#39;s Rebuttal."><span class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/Projectile.png?af216" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span><br />Blocked</span></div></div></div></div>
<ul><li>This ability will cast from wherever the caster is at the start of the cast time.</li>
<li>The damage amplification is based on the distance from <b>Nidalee's</b> location at the <i>end</i> of the cast time to the struck target's center at the time of collision.
<ul><li>The damage increase is very slightly higher than the spear's travel distance due to edge range behaviour of collisions and the distance being measured as the radius from the picked "origin" location at the end of the cast time, rather than just along the vector of the cast.</li>
<li>The damage increase does not have distinct thresholds based on the distance the spear travelled.</li>
<li>Picking Nidalee's location at the end of the cast time as the "origin" for the damage calculation may be unintended.<sup><span class="basic-tooltip" style="border-bottom:1px dotted gray;cursor:help;" title="This may not be intended.">(note)</span></sup></li></ul></li></ul>
<div style="clear:both"></div>
</div><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p>

<dl><dt><span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Arena"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Arena" title="Arena"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Arena_icon.png/20px-Arena_icon.png?c4c60" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Arena_icon.png/40px-Arena_icon.png?c4c60 2x" data-file-width="210" data-file-height="210" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Arena" title="Arena">Arena</a></span> differences <sup><a class="text" href="https://wiki.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/Template:Map_changes/data/ar?action=edit">edit</a></sup></dt>

<ul><li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Takedown" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Takedown" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/20px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/40px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Takedown">Takedown</a></span></span> minimum AD ratio changed to <span style="color:orange; white-space:normal">120% AD</span>.</li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Takedown" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Takedown" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/20px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/40px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Takedown">Takedown</a></span></span> minimum AP ratio changed to <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">80% AP</span>.<div style="clear:both"></div></li></ul>

<div class="ability-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Active:</b></span> <span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><span title="An icon representing Nidalee"><img alt="An icon representing Nidalee" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png?c6101" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png?c6101 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></span></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><strong class="selflink">Nidalee</strong></span></span> lays a <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Stealthed trap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Stealth#Stealthed_traps_and_wards" title="Stealth"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png/20px-Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png?9f6f9" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png/40px-Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png?9f6f9 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Stealth#Stealthed_traps_and_wards" title="Stealth">stealthed</a></span> that will spring upon contact with an enemy, continually dealing <span style="color: #00B0F0; white-space:normal">magic damage</span> over a few seconds.   </div><div class="ability-info-content"><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/Nidalee_Bushwhack.png?2263d" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span></div>
<div class="ability-info-description"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Active:</b></span> <b>Nidalee</b> lays a trap at the target location that becomes <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Stealthed trap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Stealth#Stealthed_traps_and_wards" title="Stealth"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png/20px-Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png?9f6f9" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png/40px-Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png?9f6f9 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Stealth#Stealthed_traps_and_wards" title="Stealth">stealthed</a></span> after arming over 1.<small>5</small> seconds, lasting for up to 120 seconds and granting <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Sight"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Sight" title="Sight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Sight_icon.png/20px-Sight_icon.png?0aaf0" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Sight_icon.png?0aaf0 2x" data-file-width="26" data-file-height="26" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Sight" title="Sight">sight</a></span> within its radius. The trap will spring upon contact with an enemy, dealing <span style="color: #00B0F0; white-space:normal">magic damage</span> every second over 4 seconds.</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats"><dl class="skill-tabs" style="letter-spacing:0.02rem;"><dt><span class="template_lc"><b>Magic Damage Per Tick:</b></span></dt><dd>10 / 20 / 30 / 40 / 50 <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">(+ 5% AP)</span></dd><dt><span class="template_lc"><b>Total Magic Damage:</b></span></dt><dd>40 / 80 / 120 / 160 / 200 <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">(+ 20% AP)</span></dd></dl></div>
</div><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"></div>
<div class="ability-info-description no-stats">Traps have <span style="color: #21B053; white-space:normal"><span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Health" title="Health"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Health_icon.png/15px-Health_icon.png?f8c57" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Health_icon.png/30px-Health_icon.png?f8c57 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;6 <b>maximum</b> health</span></span> and can only be damaged by champion <a href="/en-us/Basic_attacks" class="mw-redirect" title="Basic attacks">basic attacks</a> (2 hit points from <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Ranged"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Ranged" title="Ranged"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ranged_role.png/20px-Ranged_role.png?62375" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Ranged_role.png/40px-Ranged_role.png?62375 2x" data-file-width="168" data-file-height="168" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Ranged" class="mw-redirect" title="Ranged">ranged</a></span> and 3 hit points from <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Melee"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Melee" title="Melee"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Melee_role.png/20px-Melee_role.png?166b1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Melee_role.png/40px-Melee_role.png?166b1 2x" data-file-width="168" data-file-height="168" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Melee" class="mw-redirect" title="Melee">melee</a></span>). Up to a maximum of <span class="pp-tooltip" style="position:relative; border-bottom:1px dotted; cursor:help;" data-start="4;1" data-finish="10;16" data-bot_values="4;6;8;10" data-top_values="1;6;11;16">4 / 6 / 8 / 10 (based on level)</span> traps may be active at once.</div>

<div class="ability-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Active:</b></span> <span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><span title="An icon representing Nidalee"><img alt="An icon representing Nidalee" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png?c6101" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png?c6101 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></span></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><strong class="selflink">Nidalee</strong></span></span> revitalizes herself or the target allied champion, granting <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Attack_speed" title="Attack speed"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Attack_speed_icon.png/15px-Attack_speed_icon.png?1e55a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Attack_speed_icon.png/30px-Attack_speed_icon.png?1e55a 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<span style="color: #F5EE99; white-space:normal"><b>bonus</b> attack speed</span></span> for a few seconds and <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Healing"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Healing" title="Healing"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Heal_power_icon.png/20px-Heal_power_icon.png?e08e3" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Heal_power_icon.png/40px-Heal_power_icon.png?e08e3 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Healing" title="Healing">healing</a></span> the target based on <span style="color: #21B053; <div class="skill skill_q" style="padding: 1em; margin-top: 1em; box-shadow:black 0 2px 5px 0;color:#c8c4bd; border:#525244 solid 1px; background:#082848 no-repeat right top; overflow:hidden; position:relative; z-index: 100;">
<div id="Takedown" class="skill_header skill_wrapper"><span class="plainlinks"><a class="text" href="https://wiki.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/Template:Data_Nidalee/Takedown?action=edit"><span class="button" title="Click here to edit this ability." style="float:right; text-align:center; border-radius: 2px; position:absolute; right:13px; z-index:5"><b>&#160;Edit&#160;</b></span></a></span><div class="ability-info-container"><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_wrapper">
<div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_ability">Takedown</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_list"><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat"><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat-label"><span class="basic-tooltip" style="border-bottom:1px dotted gray;cursor:help;" title="Starts post-effect">COOLDOWN</span>:</div><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat-value">6</div></div><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat"><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat-label">CAST TIME:</div><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat-value">none</div></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ability-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Active:</b></span> <span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><span title="An icon representing Nidalee"><img alt="An icon representing Nidalee" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png?c6101" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png?c6101 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></span></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><strong class="selflink">Nidalee's</strong></span></span> next basic attack within some time will gain <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Range" title="Range"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/15px-Range_icon.png?ae16f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/30px-Range_icon.png?ae16f 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<b>bonus</b> range</span> and deal <span style="color: #00B0F0; white-space:normal">magic damage</span> based on the <span style="color: #21B053; white-space:normal">target's <b>missing</b> health</span>. <span class="template_sbc"><b><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Prowl" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Prowl" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/20px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/40px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Prowl">Hunted</a></span></span> Bonus:</b></span> A <i>Hunted</i> target hit will take <span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Damage#Successful_ability_casts" title="Damage"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Successfully_enhanced_damage_magic_icon.png/20px-Successfully_enhanced_damage_magic_icon.png?10833" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Successfully_enhanced_damage_magic_icon.png/40px-Successfully_enhanced_damage_magic_icon.png?10833 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span> <span class="basic-tooltip" style="border-bottom:1px dotted gray;cursor:help;" title="Cosmetic critical strike">increased damage</span>.  </div><div class="ability-info-content"><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span></div>
<div class="ability-info-description"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Active:</b></span> <b>Nidalee</b> empowers her next <a href="/en-us/Basic_attack" title="Basic attack">basic attack</a> within 10 seconds to have an <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Uncancellable windup"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Basic_attack#Uncancellable_Windup" title="Basic attack"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Vi_Relentless_Force_2.png/20px-Vi_Relentless_Force_2.png?9f7e9" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Vi_Relentless_Force_2.png/40px-Vi_Relentless_Force_2.png?9f7e9 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Basic_attack#Uncancellable_Windup" title="Basic attack">uncancellable windup</a></span>, gain <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Range" title="Range"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/15px-Range_icon.png?ae16f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/30px-Range_icon.png?ae16f 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;75 <b>bonus</b> range</span> and deal <span style="color: #00B0F0; white-space:normal"><b>modified</b> magic damage</span> that is increased by an amount for every <span style="color: #21B053; white-space:normal">1% of the target's <b>missing</b> health</span>.<br /><br /><i>Takedown</i> can <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Critically strike"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Critical_strike" title="Critical strike"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Critical_strike_icon.png/20px-Critical_strike_icon.png?d199f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Critical_strike_icon.png/40px-Critical_strike_icon.png?d199f 2x" data-file-width="144" data-file-height="144" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Critical_strike" title="Critical strike">critically strike</a></span> for <span style="color: #B4814C; white-space:normal">(75%&#160;+&#160;<span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Infinity Edge" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Infinity_Edge" title="An icon for the item Infinity Edge"><img alt="An icon for the item Infinity Edge" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Infinity_Edge_item.png/20px-Infinity_Edge_item.png?71b4c" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Infinity_Edge_item.png/40px-Infinity_Edge_item.png?71b4c 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Infinity_Edge" title="Infinity Edge">40%</a></span></span>)</span> <span style="color:orange; white-space:normal">AD</span> <span style="color: #00B0F0; white-space:normal"><b>bonus</b> magic damage</span>.</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats"><span class="template_sbc"><b><i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Takedown" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Takedown" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/20px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/40px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Takedown">Takedown</a></span></span></i> scales with <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Aspect of the Cougar" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Aspect_of_the_Cougar" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Aspect of the Cougar"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Aspect of the Cougar" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png/20px-Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png?890a1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png/40px-Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png?890a1 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Aspect_of_the_Cougar">Aspect of the Cougar's</a></span></span></i> rank</b></span>
<dl class="skill-tabs" style="letter-spacing:0.02rem;"><dt><span class="template_lc"><b>Minimum Magic Damage:</b></span></dt><dd>5 / 30 / 55 / 80 <span style="color:orange; white-space:normal">(+ 75% AD)</span> <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">(+ 40% AP)</span></dd><dt><span class="template_lc"><b>Maximum Magic Damage:</b></span></dt><dd>10 / 67.<small>5</small> / 137.<small>5</small> / 220 <span style="color:orange; white-space:normal">(+ 150 / 168.<small>75</small> / 187.<small>5</small> / 206.<small>25</small>% AD)</span> <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">(+ 80 / 90 / 100 / 110% AP)</span></dd></dl>
<dl class="skill-tabs" style="letter-spacing:0.02rem;"><dt><span class="template_lc"><b>Increased Damage Modifier:</b></span></dt><dd>1 / 1.<small>25</small> / 1.<small>5</small> / 1.<small>75</small>%</dd><dt><span class="template_lc"><b>Maximum Increased Damage:</b></span></dt><dd>100 / 125 / 150 / 175%</dd></dl></div>
</div><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"></div>
<div class="ability-info-description"><span class="template_sbc"><b><i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Prowl" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Prowl" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/20px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/40px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Prowl">Hunt</a></span></span></i> Bonus:</b></span> Hitting a <i>Hunted</i> target <span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Damage#Successful_ability_casts" title="Damage"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Successfully_enhanced_damage_magic_icon.png/20px-Successfully_enhanced_damage_magic_icon.png?10833" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Successfully_enhanced_damage_magic_icon.png/40px-Successfully_enhanced_damage_magic_icon.png?10833 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span> <span class="basic-tooltip" style="border-bottom:1px dotted gray;cursor:help;" title="Cosmetic critical strike">increases</span> <i>Takedown's</i> damage by 30%.</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats"><dl class="skill-tabs" style="letter-spacing:0.02rem;"><dt><span class="template_lc"><b><i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Prowl" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Prowl" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/20px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/40px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Prowl">Prowl</a></span></span></i>-Enhanced Minimum Damage:</b></span></dt><dd>6.<small>5</small> / 39 / 71.<small>5</small> / 104 <span style="color:orange; </div><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"></div>
<div class="ability-info-description no-stats"><i>Takedown <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Basic attack reset"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Basic_attack#Attack_reset" title="Basic attack"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Fiora_Bladework.png/20px-Fiora_Bladework.png?1fcc5" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Fiora_Bladework.png/40px-Fiora_Bladework.png?1fcc5 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Basic_attack#Attack_reset" title="Basic attack">resets</a></span> <b>Nidalee's</b> basic attack timer. Other damage converted to <span style="color: #00B0F0; white-space:normal">magic damage</span> by Takedown are not increased by Takedown's respective effects. <b>Nidalee</b> loses Takedown's empowered attack immediately when she switches to <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Aspect of the Cougar" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Aspect_of_the_Cougar" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Aspect of the Cougar"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Aspect of the Cougar" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png/20px-Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png?890a1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png/40px-Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png?890a1 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Aspect_of_the_Cougar">Human Form</a></span></span>.</i></div>

<div style="padding:0.5em 1em;"><div class="infobox"><div class="infobox-section-stacked"><div class="infobox-data-row"><div class="infobox-data-label">Targeting input</div><div class="infobox-data-value"><a href="/en-us/Targeting#Auto" title="Targeting">Auto</a></div></div></div><div class="infobox-header">Damage classification</div><div class="infobox-section-cell"><div class="infobox-data-row"><div class="infobox-data-label">Type</div><div class="infobox-data-value"><span title="This ability applies multiple effect classifications. See the notes for more details."><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Jhin_Deadly_Flourish.png/56px-Jhin_Deadly_Flourish.png?473eb" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="56" height="56" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Jhin_Deadly_Flourish.png?473eb 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span><br />See Notes</span></div></div><div class="infobox-data-row"><div class="infobox-data-label">Sub-type(s)</div><div class="infobox-data-value"><span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Magic damage"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Magic_damage" title="Magic damage"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Magic_damage.png/56px-Magic_damage.png?2db19" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="56" height="56" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Magic_damage.png/112px-Magic_damage.png?2db19 2x" data-file-width="163" data-file-height="163" /></a></span><br /><a href="/en-us/Magic_damage" title="Magic damage">Magic</a></span></div></div></div><div class="infobox-header">Counters</div><div class="infobox-section-cell"><div class="infobox-data-row"><div class="infobox-data-label">Spell shield</div><div class="infobox-data-value"><span title="This ability will be blocked by spell shields. • Edge of Night • Banshee&#39;s Veil • Nocturne&#39;s Shroud of Darkness • Sivir&#39;s Spell Shield"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Sivir_Spell_Shield.png/56px-Sivir_Spell_Shield.png?4c4d1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="56" height="56" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Sivir_Spell_Shield.png?4c4d1 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span><br />Blocked</span></div></div><div class="infobox-data-row"><div class="infobox-data-label">Parries</div><div class="infobox-data-value"><span class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Missing_role.png/66px-Missing_role.png?f30f7" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="66" height="56" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Missing_role.png/132px-Missing_role.png?f30f7 2x" data-file-width="500" data-file-height="423" /></span></span><br />Missing</div></div></div></div>
<ul><li><i>Takedown's</i> attack deals <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Basic damage"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Damage" title="Damage"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Basic_Attack.png/20px-Basic_Attack.png?66a25" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Basic_Attack.png/40px-Basic_Attack.png?66a25 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Damage" title="Damage">basic damage</a></span>, but also triggers spell effects by also being tagged as <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Spell damage"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Damage" title="Damage"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Annie_Disintegrate.png/20px-Annie_Disintegrate.png?bbde6" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Annie_Disintegrate.png/40px-Annie_Disintegrate.png?bbde6 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Damage" title="Damage">spell damage</a></span>.</li>
<li><i>Takedown's</i> damage is not affected by <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Critical strike"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Critical_strike" title="Critical strike"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Critical_strike_icon.png/20px-Critical_strike_icon.png?d199f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Critical_strike_icon.png/40px-Critical_strike_icon.png?d199f 2x" data-file-width="144" data-file-height="144" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Critical_strike" title="Critical strike">critical strike</a></span> modifiers, but the basic attack can still critically strike and the <b>bonus</b> damage from the critical strike is converted to <span style="color: #00B0F0; white-space:normal">magic damage</span>.
<ul><li><i>Takedown's</i> damage modifier does not affect the <b>bonus</b> damage dealt by the critical strike.</li></ul></li>
<li><i>Takedown</i> converts the <b>bonus</b> damage dealt by <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Spellblade"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Named_item_effect#Spellblade" title="Named item effect"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Sheen_item.png/20px-Sheen_item.png?2bece" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Sheen_item.png/40px-Sheen_item.png?2bece 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Named_item_effect#Spellblade" title="Named item effect">Spellblade</a></span> to <span style="color: #00B0F0; white-space:normal">magic damage</span> from <span style="color: #FF8C34; white-space:normal">physical</span>, but does not apply its damage modifier to the effect.</li>
<li><i>Takedown's</i> damage will apply <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Life_steal" title="Life steal"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Life_steal_icon.png/15px-Life_steal_icon.png?e8287" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Life_steal_icon.png/30px-Life_steal_icon.png?e8287 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<a href="/en-us/Life_steal" title="Life steal">life steal</a></span>.</li>
<li><i>Takedown's</i> damage modifier does not apply against structures; the minimum damage is always applied.</li>
<li><span style="color:red; font-family:math; font-weight:bold; font-size:1em;" title="Pending for test"><span class="fas fa-vial"></span>PENDING FOR TEST:</span> - Parry interactions (<span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Dodge"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Attack_effects#Parrying" title="Attack effects"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Jax_Counter_Strike_old.png/20px-Jax_Counter_Strike_old.png?95754" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Jax_Counter_Strike_old.png/40px-Jax_Counter_Strike_old.png?95754 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Attack_effects#Parrying" title="Attack effects">dodge</a></span>, <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Block"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Attack_effects#Parrying" title="Attack effects"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Shen_Spirit%27s_Refuge.png/20px-Shen_Spirit%27s_Refuge.png?319df" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Shen_Spirit%27s_Refuge.png/40px-Shen_Spirit%27s_Refuge.png?319df 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Attack_effects#Parrying" title="Attack effects">block</a></span> and <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Blind"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Blind" title="Blind"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Blind_icon.png/20px-Blind_icon.png?b97a1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Blind_icon.png/40px-Blind_icon.png?b97a1 2x" data-file-width="65" data-file-height="65" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Blind" class="mw-redirect" title="Blind">blind</a></span>).</li></ul>
<div style="clear:both"></div>
</div><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p>
			</div>

<dl><dt><span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Arena"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Arena" title="Arena"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Arena_icon.png/20px-Arena_icon.png?c4c60" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Arena_icon.png/40px-Arena_icon.png?c4c60 2x" data-file-width="210" data-file-height="210" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Arena" title="Arena">Arena</a></span> differences <sup><a class="text" href="https://wiki.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/Template:Map_changes/data/ar?action=edit">edit</a></sup></dt>

<li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Takedown" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Takedown" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/20px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/40px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Takedown">Takedown</a></span></span> minimum AP ratio changed to <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">80% AP</span>.<div style="clear:both"></div></li></ul>

<div id="Pounce" class="skill_header skill_wrapper"><span class="plainlinks"><a class="text" href="https://wiki.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/Template:Data_Nidalee/Pounce?action=edit"><span class="button" title="Click here to edit this ability." style="float:right; text-align:center; border-radius: 2px; position:absolute; right:13px; z-index:5"><b>&#160;Edit&#160;</b></span></a></span><div class="ability-info-container"><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_wrapper">
<div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_ability">Pounce</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_list"><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat"><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat-label">COOLDOWN:</div><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat-value"><span class="basic-tooltip" style="border-bottom:1px dotted gray;cursor:help;" title="Starts on cast">6</span></div></div><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat"><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat-label">CAST TIME:</div><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat-value">none</div></div><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat"><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat-label">TARGET RANGE:</div><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat-value"><span class="basic-tooltip" style="border-bottom:1px dotted gray;cursor:help;" title="Standard range">375</span> / <span class="basic-tooltip" style="border-bottom:1px dotted gray;cursor:help;" title="Enhanced range">750</span></div></div><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat"><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat-label">EFFECT RADIUS:</div><div class="ability-info-stats&#95;_stat-value">200 / 250</div></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ability-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Passive:</b></span> Killing an enemy or using <i>Pounce's</i> <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Prowl" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Prowl" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/20px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/40px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Prowl">Hunted</a></span></span></i> bonus will <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Cooldown_reduction" title="Cooldown reduction"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Cooldown_reduction_icon.png/15px-Cooldown_reduction_icon.png?27276" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Cooldown_reduction_icon.png/30px-Cooldown_reduction_icon.png?27276 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;reduce</span> <i>Pounce's</i> cooldown. <span class="template_sbc"><b>Active:</b></span> <span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><span title="An icon representing Nidalee"><img alt="An icon representing Nidalee" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png?c6101" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png?c6101 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></span></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><strong class="selflink">Nidalee</strong></span></span> dashes in the target direction, dealing <span style="color: #00B0F0; white-space:normal">magic damage</span> to nearby enemies upon arrival. <span class="template_sbc"><b><i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Prowl" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Prowl" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/20px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/40px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Prowl">Hunted</a></span></span></i> Bonus:</b></span> <i>Pounce</i> has increased range when cast near <i>Hunted</i> targets. </div><div class="ability-info-content"><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"></div>
<div class="ability-info-description"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Passive:</b></span> Killing an enemy while in <i>Cougar Form</i> or using <i>Pounce's Hunt</i> bonus reduces <i>Pounce's</i> <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Cooldown" title="Cooldown"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Cooldown_icon.png/15px-Cooldown_icon.png?50d14" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Cooldown_icon.png?50d14 2x" data-file-width="20" data-file-height="20" /></a></span>&#160;<b>current</b> cooldown</span> to a minimum value.</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats"><span class="template_sbc"><b><i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Pounce" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Pounce" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Pounce"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Pounce" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Pounce.png/20px-Nidalee_Pounce.png?b56c7" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Pounce.png/40px-Nidalee_Pounce.png?b56c7 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Pounce">Pounce</a></span></span></i> scales with <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Aspect of the Cougar" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Aspect_of_the_Cougar" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Aspect of the Cougar"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Aspect of the Cougar" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png/20px-Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png?890a1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png/40px-Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png?890a1 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Aspect_of_the_Cougar">Aspect of the Cougar's</a></span></span></i> rank</b></span>
<dl class="skill-tabs" style="letter-spacing:0.02rem;"><dt><span class="template_lc"><b>Reduced Cooldown:</b></span></dt><dd><span class="basic-tooltip" style="border-bottom:1px dotted gray;cursor:help;" title="Affected by ability haste">3 / 2.<small>5</small> / 2 / 1.<small>5</small> seconds</span></dd></dl></div>
</div><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/Nidalee_Pounce.png?b56c7" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span></div>
<div class="ability-info-description"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Active:</b></span> <b>Nidalee</b> <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Dash"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Dash" title="Dash"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Dash.png/20px-Dash.png?e5c61" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Dash.png/40px-Dash.png?e5c61 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Dash" title="Dash">leaps</a></span> a fixed distance in the target direction. Upon arrival, she deals <span style="color: #00B0F0; white-space:normal">magic damage</span> to nearby enemies.</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats"><dl class="skill-tabs" style="letter-spacing:0.02rem;"><dt><span class="template_lc"><b>Magic Damage:</b></span></dt><dd>55 / 100 / 145 / 190 <span style="color:orange; white-space:normal">(+ 50% <b>bonus</b> AD)</span> <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">(+ 30% AP)</span></dd></dl></div>
</div><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"></div>
<div class="ability-info-description no-stats"><span class="template_sbc"><b><i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Prowl" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Prowl" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/20px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/40px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Prowl">Hunted</a></span></span></i> Bonus:</b></span> <b>Nidalee</b> can perform <i>Pounce</i> from an increased range on a <i>Hunted</i> enemy closest to the cursor. She will leap to the front of the target.</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats"></div>

<div class="ability-info-icon"></div>
<div class="ability-info-description no-stats"><i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Takedown" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Takedown" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/20px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/40px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Takedown">Takedown</a></span></span> and <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Aspect of the Cougar" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Aspect_of_the_Cougar" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Aspect of the Cougar"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Aspect of the Cougar" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png/20px-Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png?890a1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png/40px-Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png?890a1 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Aspect_of_the_Cougar">Aspect of the Cougar</a></span></span> can be cast during the dash.</i></div>

<li>Casting <i>Pounce</i> on a <i>Hunted</i> target will extend the remaining duration of their <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Prowl" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Prowl" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/20px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/40px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Prowl">Hunted</a></span></span></i> debuff by 1.<small>5</small> seconds, up to the original duration.</li></ul>
