<div class="ability-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Active:</b></span> <span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><span title="An icon representing Nidalee"><img alt="An icon representing Nidalee" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png?c6101" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Nidalee_OriginalSquare.png?c6101 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></span></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><strong class="selflink">Nidalee</strong></span></span> switches between her <b>Human Form</b> and <b>Cougar Form</b>. <span class="template_sbc"><b><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png/20px-Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png?890a1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png/40px-Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png?890a1 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span> Cougar Form:</b></span> <b>Nidalee</b> transforms into a cougar, gaining <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Melee"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Melee" title="Melee"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Melee_role.png/20px-Melee_role.png?166b1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Melee_role.png/40px-Melee_role.png?166b1 2x" data-file-width="168" data-file-height="168" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Melee" class="mw-redirect" title="Melee">melee</a></span> attacks and access to her cougar abilities. <span class="template_sbc"><b><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar_2.png/20px-Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar_2.png?62ff3" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar_2.png/40px-Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar_2.png?62ff3 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span> Human Form:</b></span> <b>Nidalee</b> transforms into a human, gaining <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Ranged"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Ranged" title="Ranged"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ranged_role.png/20px-Ranged_role.png?62375" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Ranged_role.png/40px-Ranged_role.png?62375 2x" data-file-width="168" data-file-height="168" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Ranged" class="mw-redirect" title="Ranged">ranged</a></span> attacks and access to her human abilities. While in <b>Human Form</b>, applying a <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Prowl" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Prowl" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/20px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/40px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Prowl">Hunted</a></span></span></i> mark will <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Cooldown_reduction" title="Cooldown reduction"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Cooldown_reduction_icon.png/15px-Cooldown_reduction_icon.png?27276" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Cooldown_reduction_icon.png/30px-Cooldown_reduction_icon.png?27276 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;reset</span> <i>Aspect of the Cougar's</i> cooldown. <b>Nidalee</b> begins with one rank in <i>Aspect of the Cougar</i>. <b>Cougar Form's</b> abilities scale based on <i>Aspect of the Cougar's</i> rank.</div><div class="ability-info-content"><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"></div>
<div class="ability-info-description no-stats"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Active:</b></span> <b>Nidalee</b> switches between her <span class="template_sbc"><b>Human Form</b></span> and <span class="template_sbc"><b>Cougar Form</b></span>.</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats"></div>
</div><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar.png?890a1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span></div>
<div class="ability-info-description no-stats"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Cougar Form:</b></span> <b>Nidalee</b> transforms into a cougar, gaining <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Melee"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Melee" title="Melee"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Melee_role.png/20px-Melee_role.png?166b1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Melee_role.png/40px-Melee_role.png?166b1 2x" data-file-width="168" data-file-height="168" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Melee" class="mw-redirect" title="Melee">melee</a></span> attacks with <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Range" title="Range"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/15px-Range_icon.png?ae16f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/30px-Range_icon.png?ae16f 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;125 range</span> and access to her cougar abilities.</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats"></div>
</div><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/Nidalee_Aspect_of_the_Cougar_2.png?62ff3" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span></div>
<div class="ability-info-description no-stats"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Human Form:</b></span> <b>Nidalee</b> transforms into a human, gaining <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Ranged"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Ranged" title="Ranged"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ranged_role.png/20px-Ranged_role.png?62375" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Ranged_role.png/40px-Ranged_role.png?62375 2x" data-file-width="168" data-file-height="168" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Ranged" class="mw-redirect" title="Ranged">ranged</a></span> attacks with <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Range" title="Range"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/15px-Range_icon.png?ae16f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/30px-Range_icon.png?ae16f 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;525 range</span> and access to her human abilities. While in this form, applying a <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Prowl" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Prowl" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/20px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/40px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Prowl">Hunted</a></span></span></i> mark will reset <i>Aspect of the Cougar's</i> <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Cooldown" title="Cooldown"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Cooldown_icon.png/15px-Cooldown_icon.png?50d14" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Cooldown_icon.png?50d14 2x" data-file-width="20" data-file-height="20" /></a></span>&#160;cooldown</span>.</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats"></div>
</div><div class="ability-info-row">
<div class="ability-info-icon"></div>
<div class="ability-info-description no-stats"><b>Nidalee</b> begins with one rank in <i>Aspect of the Cougar</i> and can increase it at levels 6, 11, and 16. <span class="template_sbc"><b>Cougar Form's</b></span> abilities scale based on <i>Aspect of the Cougar's</i> rank.</div>
<div class="ability-info-stats"></div>

<div class="infobox"><div class="infobox-title"><span style="font-size:large">Spring Trap</span><div style="float:right;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Bushwhack.png/48px-Nidalee_Bushwhack.png?2263d" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="48" height="48" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Nidalee_Bushwhack.png?2263d 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span></div></div><div class="infobox-image"><span class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/File:Nidalee_Trap_Render.png" class="mw-file-description"><img src="/en-us/images/Nidalee_Trap_Render.png?10aad" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="734" height="463" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="734" data-file-height="463" /></a></span></div><div class="infobox-header">Statistics</div><div class="infobox-section-column"><div class="infobox-data-row"><div class="infobox-data-label"><a href="/en-us/Health" title="Health">Health</a></div><div class="infobox-data-value">6</div></div><div class="infobox-data-row"><div class="infobox-data-label"><a href="/en-us/Damage_modifier" title="Damage modifier">Incoming damage modifier</a></div><div class="infobox-data-value">
<ul><li>2 from <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Ranged"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Ranged" title="Ranged"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ranged_role.png/20px-Ranged_role.png?62375" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Ranged_role.png/40px-Ranged_role.png?62375 2x" data-file-width="168" data-file-height="168" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Ranged" class="mw-redirect" title="Ranged">ranged</a></span> and 3 from <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Melee"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Melee" title="Melee"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Melee_role.png/20px-Melee_role.png?166b1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Melee_role.png/40px-Melee_role.png?166b1 2x" data-file-width="168" data-file-height="168" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Melee" class="mw-redirect" title="Melee">melee</a></span> champion basic attacks    </li></ul></div></div></div></div>

<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="vertical-align:top;">
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_2">Abilities</span></h3>
<dl><dt>Stealth Trap</dt></dl>
<p>The trap <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Stealthed trap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Stealth#Stealthed_traps_and_wards" title="Stealth"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png/20px-Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png?9f6f9" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png/40px-Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png?9f6f9 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Stealth#Stealthed_traps_and_wards" title="Stealth">stealths</a></span> and becomes <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Untargetable"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Untargetable" title="Untargetable"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Untargetable_icon.png/20px-Untargetable_icon.png?c022c" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Untargetable_icon.png/40px-Untargetable_icon.png?c022c 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Untargetable" class="mw-redirect" title="Untargetable">untargetable</a></span> after 1.<small>5</small> seconds, remaining vulnerable to trap-revealing effects at all times.
</p>
<dl><dt>Trap Limitation</dt></dl>
<p>Only up to <span class="pp-tooltip" style="position:relative; border-bottom:1px dotted; cursor:help;" data-start="4;1" data-finish="10;16" data-bot_values="4;6;8;10" data-top_values="1;6;11;16">4 / 6 / 8 / 10 (based on level)</span> traps may be active at once.
</p>
<dl><dt>Toxin</dt></dl>
<p>If an enemy walks over the spring trap, they are inflicted with a toxin that deals them <span style="color: #00B0F0; white-space:normal">40 / 80 / 120 / 160 / 200</span> <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">(+ 20% AP)</span> <span style="color: #00B0F0; white-space:normal"><b>total</b> magic damage</span> over 4 seconds. Additionally, they become marked as <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Prowl" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Prowl" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/20px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/40px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Prowl"><i>Hunted</i></a></span></span> for the same duration if they were a monster or champion and <b>Nidalee</b> was nearby.
</p>
</td></tr>

</tbody></table>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Patch_history">Patch history</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/en-us/Nidalee?section=4&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Patch history">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/en-us/Nidalee?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Patch history">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<dl><dd><i>For the expanded patch notes, see <a href="/en-us/Nidalee/Patch_history" title="Nidalee/Patch history">here</a>.</i></dd></dl>
<div style="overflow:auto; max-height:500px; width:auto; margin:3px 0; border:1px solid var(--league-grey-2); padding:0 0.5em 0 0.5em; box-sizing:border-box; -moz-box-sizing:border-box; -moz-border-radius-topleft:0.5em; background:var(--body-mid); border-radius:4px;">
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/V25.13" title="V25.13">V25.13</a></dt></dl>
<ul><li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Javelin Toss" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Javelin_Toss" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Javelin Toss"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Javelin Toss" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png/20px-Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png?9d69e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png/40px-Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png?9d69e 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Javelin_Toss">Javelin Toss</a></span></span>
<ul><li>Damage modifier increased to <span class="pp-tooltip" style="position:relative; border-bottom:1px dotted; cursor:help;" data-top_label="distance traveled" data-start="0;525" data-finish="225;1300" data-bot_values="0;45;90;135;180;225" data-top_values="525;680;835;990;1145;1300" data-bot_key="%">0% – 225% (based on distance traveled)</span> from <span class="pp-tooltip" style="position:relative; border-bottom:1px dotted; cursor:help;" data-top_label="distance traveled" data-start="0;525" data-finish="200;1300" data-bot_values="0;40;80;120;160;200" data-top_values="525;680;835;990;1145;1300" data-bot_key="%">0% – 200%</span>.
<ul><li>Maximum base damage increased to 227.<small>5</small> / 292.<small>5</small> / 357.<small>5</small> / 422.<small>5</small> / 487.<small>5</small> from 210 / 270 / 330 / 390 / 450.</li>
<li>Maximum AP ratio increased to <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">162.<small>5</small>% AP</span> from <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">150% AP</span>.</li></ul></li></ul></li></ul>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/V25.12" title="V25.12">V25.12</a></dt></dl>
<ul><li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Swipe" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Swipe" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Swipe"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Swipe" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Swipe.png/20px-Nidalee_Swipe.png?858cd" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Swipe.png/40px-Nidalee_Swipe.png?858cd 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Swipe">Swipe</a></span></span>
<ul><li>AP ratio increased to <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">55% AP</span> from <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">40% AP</span>.</li></ul></li></ul>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/V25.S1.1" title="V25.S1.1">V25.S1.1</a></dt></dl>
<ul><li>General
<ul><li>Now swaps <span class="inline-image label-after rune-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-rune="Axiom Arcanist" data-game="lol"><span style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Axiom_Arcanist" title="An icon representing Axiom Arcanist"><img alt="An icon representing Axiom Arcanist" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Axiom_Arcanist_rune.png/20px-Axiom_Arcanist_rune.png?f0a6e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Axiom_Arcanist_rune.png/40px-Axiom_Arcanist_rune.png?f0a6e 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="word-break: keep-all;"><a href="/en-us/Axiom_Arcanist" title="Axiom Arcanist">Axiom Arcanist</a></span></span> with <span class="inline-image label-after rune-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-rune="Nimbus Cloak" data-game="lol"><span style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nimbus_Cloak" title="An icon representing Nimbus Cloak"><img alt="An icon representing Nimbus Cloak" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nimbus_Cloak_rune.png/20px-Nimbus_Cloak_rune.png?4c7ce" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nimbus_Cloak_rune.png/40px-Nimbus_Cloak_rune.png?4c7ce 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="word-break: keep-all;"><a href="/en-us/Nimbus_Cloak" title="Nimbus Cloak">Nimbus Cloak</a></span></span>.</li></ul></li></ul>

<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/V4.10" title="V4.10">V4.10</a></dt></dl>
<ul><li>Gameplay Update
<ul><li>General
<ul><li>Basic attack timing updated.</li>
<li>New ability icons.</li>
<li><span class="template_sbc"><b>New Effect:</b></span> Death Recap differentiates between human and cougar abilities.</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Prowl" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Prowl" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/20px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/40px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Prowl">Prowl</a></span></span>
<ul><li>In-brush bonus movement speed reduced to 10% from 15.</li>
<li><span class="template_sbc"><b>New Effect:</b></span> In-brush bonus movement speed increases to 30% while moving toward a visible enemy champion within 5500 range.</li>
<li><span class="template_sbc"><b>New Effect - Hunt:</b></span> Damaging enemy champions with <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Javelin Toss" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Javelin_Toss" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Javelin Toss"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Javelin Toss" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png/20px-Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png?9d69e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png/40px-Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png?9d69e 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Javelin_Toss">Javelin Toss</a></span></span> and <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Bushwhack" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Bushwhack" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Bushwhack"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Bushwhack" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Bushwhack.png/20px-Nidalee_Bushwhack.png?2263d" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Bushwhack.png/40px-Nidalee_Bushwhack.png?2263d 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Bushwhack">Bushwhack</a></span></span> marks them as Hunted for 4 seconds, granting Nidalee sight of them. Nidalee ignores unit collision and gains 30% bonus movement speed while moving toward marked targets, and her next cougar ability against them consumes the mark for an enhanced effect.</li>
<li>New Hunted particle.</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Javelin Toss" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Javelin_Toss" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Javelin Toss"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Javelin Toss" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png/20px-Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png?9d69e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png/40px-Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png?9d69e 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Javelin_Toss">Javelin Toss</a></span></span>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/en-us/Nidalee?section=5&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Trivia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/en-us/Nidalee?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Trivia">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Nidalee is the first champion to have more than 4 active <a href="/en-us/Abilities" class="mw-redirect" title="Abilities">abilities</a>.</li>
<li>Nidalee, <span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Elise" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" Elise" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Elise_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Elise_OriginalSquare.png?b97b0" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Elise_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Elise_OriginalSquare.png?b97b0 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Elise" title="Elise">Elise</a></span></span>, <span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Gnar" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Gnar" title="An icon representing Gnar"><img alt="An icon representing Gnar" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Gnar_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Gnar_OriginalSquare.png?11c50" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Gnar_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Gnar_OriginalSquare.png?11c50 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Kayle" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" href="/en-us/Kayle" title="Kayle">Kayle</a></span></span> are the only champions to be conditionally considered both <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Ranged"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Ranged" title="Ranged"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ranged_role.png/20px-Ranged_role.png?62375" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Swain" title="An icon representing Swain"><img alt="An icon representing Swain" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Swain_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Swain_OriginalSquare.png?b7cdb" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Swain_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Swain_OriginalSquare.png?b7cdb 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Swain" title="Swain">Swain</a></span></span>).</li>
<li>Nidalee has four different running animations (human run, human <a href="/en-us/Brush" title="Brush">brush</a> sprint, cougar run, cougar brush sprint).</li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Pounce" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Pounce" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Pounce"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Pounce" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Pounce.png/20px-Nidalee_Pounce.png?b56c7" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Pounce.png/40px-Nidalee_Pounce.png?b56c7 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Pounce">Pounce</a></span></span> was the first ability to feature a static cooldown (was removed in <a href="/en-us/V1.0.0.124" title="V1.0.0.124">V1.0.0.124</a>).</li>
<li>Nidalee used to have a <a href="/en-us/Easter_egg" title="Easter egg">hidden passive</a> where nearby allied champions gain <span style="color: #A560EB; white-space:normal"><span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Experience_(champion)" title="Experience (champion)"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Experience_icon.png/15px-Experience_icon.png?8a0e8" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Experience_icon.png?8a0e8 2x" data-file-width="18" data-file-height="18" /></a></span>&#160;5 <b>bonus</b> experience</span></span> <a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=qQ2iCh6wGHA">every 5 seconds</a> if Nidalee is <a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cougar_(slang)">higher-leveled</a> (a double-entendre).</li>
<li>In older versions of the game, <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Javelin Toss" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Javelin_Toss" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Javelin Toss"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Javelin Toss" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png/20px-Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png?9d69e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png/40px-Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png?9d69e 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Javelin_Toss">Javelin Toss</a></span></span> was the highest-damage single-hit spell in the game.</li>
<li>Nidalee was deemed overpowered in the <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Ultra rapid fire"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Ultra_Rapid_Fire" title="Ultra Rapid Fire"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/The_Thinking_Manatee_profileicon.png/20px-The_Thinking_Manatee_profileicon.png?81148" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/The_Thinking_Manatee_profileicon.png/40px-The_Thinking_Manatee_profileicon.png?81148 2x" data-file-width="300" data-file-height="300" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Ultra_Rapid_Fire" title="Ultra Rapid Fire">Ultra Rapid Fire</a></span> game mode (2014 edition) and was ultimately disabled in non-custom games.</li>
<li>After her visual rework, her feline forms received morphological features from cougars' <a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pantherinae">bigger relatives</a>, like mane, higher shoulders than haunches, long skull &amp; jaws, &amp; occasionally long fangs of <a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Machairodontinae">sabre-toothed cats</a> and other <a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barbourofelidae">cat-like</a> <a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nimravidae">relatives</a>.</li>
<li>Nidalee is one of the first champions to have one skin for each of the three big annual events of the year: <a href="/en-us/Lunar_Revel" class="mw-redirect" title="Lunar Revel">Lunar Revel</a>, <a href="/en-us/Harrowing" class="mw-redirect" title="Harrowing">Harrowing</a>, <a href="/en-us/Snowdown_Showdown" title="Snowdown Showdown">Snowdown Showdown</a>. She received her <span style="white-space:pre"><span class="inline-image label-after skin-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-skin="Warring Kingdoms" data-champion="Nidalee" data-game="lol"><span style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee/Cosmetics" title="An icon representing Nidalee&#39;s Warring Kingdoms skin in League of Legends"><img alt="An icon representing Nidalee&#39;s Warring Kingdoms skin in League of Legends" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_WarringKingdomsCircle.png/20px-Nidalee_WarringKingdomsCircle.png?6699d" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_WarringKingdomsCircle.png/40px-Nidalee_WarringKingdomsCircle.png?6699d 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee/Cosmetics" title="Nidalee/Cosmetics">Warring Kingdoms</a></span></span></span> skin alongside <span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Katarina" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Katarina" title="An icon representing Katarina"><img alt="An icon representing Katarina" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Katarina_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Katarina_OriginalSquare.png?e11e0" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Katarina_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Katarina_OriginalSquare.png?e11e0 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Katarina" title="Katarina">Katarina's</a></span></span> in <a href="/en-us/Warring_Kingdoms_(Universe)" class="mw-redirect" title="Warring Kingdoms (Universe)">Warring Kingdoms 2015</a>.</li>
<li>Given that she is a <a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/feral_child">wild child</a>, it is unknown how Nidalee could have learnt to speak languages fluently; since in the real world, feral humans who learn their first language <a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Critical_Period">late in life</a> never master the linguistic aspects of phonology, morphology, and syntax.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/en-us/Nidalee?section=6&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: See also">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/en-us/Nidalee?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: See also">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
