<li><span class="inline-image unit-icon label-after" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param=""><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Seth" title="An icon representing Seth"><img alt="An icon representing Seth" src="/en-us/images/thumb/SethSquare.png/20px-SethSquare.png?01c9a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/SethSquare.png/40px-SethSquare.png?01c9a 2x" data-file-width="146" data-file-height="146" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Seth" class="mw-redirect" title="Seth">Seth</a></span></span></li>
<li><span class="inline-image unit-icon label-after" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param=""><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Tabu" title="An icon representing Tabu"><img alt="An icon representing Tabu" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Tabu_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Tabu_OriginalSquare.png?cd7af" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Tabu_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Tabu_OriginalSquare.png?cd7af 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Tabu" title="Tabu">Tabu</a></span></span></li>
<li><span class="inline-image unit-icon label-after" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param=""><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Tiki" title="An icon representing Tiki"><img alt="An icon representing Tiki" src="/en-us/images/thumb/TikiSquare.png/20px-TikiSquare.png?b4890" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/TikiSquare.png/40px-TikiSquare.png?b4890 2x" data-file-width="146" data-file-height="146" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Tiki" class="mw-redirect" title="Tiki">Tiki</a></span></span></li>
<li><span class="inline-image unit-icon label-after" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param=""><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Urf" title="An icon representing Urf"><img alt="An icon representing Urf" src="/en-us/images/thumb/UrfSquare.png/20px-UrfSquare.png?6d852" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/UrfSquare.png/40px-UrfSquare.png?6d852 2x" data-file-width="133" data-file-height="137" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Urf" class="mw-redirect" title="Urf">Urf</a></span></span></li>
<li><span class="inline-image unit-icon label-after" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param=""><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Well" title="An icon representing Well"><img alt="An icon representing Well" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Well_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Well_OriginalSquare.png?d96f0" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Well_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Well_OriginalSquare.png?d96f0 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Well" title="Well">Well</a></span></span></li></ul>
</div>
</td></tr>
</tbody></table></div>
</div><div class="hidden-metadata navigation-not-searchable"><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Attack windup</span></div>
The <b>attack windup</b> is a portion of the <span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/File:Basic_attack_icon.png" class="mw-file-description"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Basic_attack_icon.png/16px-Basic_attack_icon.png?879ff" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="16" height="16" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Basic_attack_icon.png?879ff 2x" data-file-width="32" data-file-height="32" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Basic_attack" title="Basic attack">basic attack</a> animation that must play out in order to launch it. For <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Projectile"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Projectile" title="Projectile"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Projectile.png/20px-Projectile.png?af216" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Projectile.png/40px-Projectile.png?af216 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Projectile" title="Projectile">projectile</a></span> basic attacks, the windup usually aligns with drawing the projectile on-screen.<hr style="width:90%; border:solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25); border-width:0px 0px 1px 0px;" />
<p>
The attack windup is displayed as a percentage, and any windup modifier is listed as a decimal next to it.</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Attack speed ratio</span></div>
<p>The <b>Attack speed ratio (AS ratio)</b> adjusts the effectiveness of bonus AS from all sources. It is usually equal to the unit's base AS (level 1 with no bonuses), but tuning to a higher or lower relative value translates to more or less bonus AS received compared to other units with the same base AS. 
</p>
<center><big>Total AS&#160;=&#160;Base AS&#160;+&#160;Bonus AS&#160;&#215;&#160;<span style="color: #D929D9; white-space:normal"><b>AS Ratio</b></span></big><br /><i>(All values in decimal form)</i></center><hr style="width:90%; border:solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25); border-width:0px 0px 1px 0px;" />
<p>
The ingame stats HUD displays the <b>AS ratio</b> instead of base AS to communicate this comparative effectiveness. The Wiki opts to always list both stats and show the <b>AS ratio</b> as "N/A" if the two are equal.</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Gameplay_radius.png/44px-Gameplay_radius.png?ee4af" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Gameplay_radius.png?ee4af 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Gameplay radius</span></div>
<p>A unit's <b>gameplay radius</b> is a <a href="/en-us/Champion_statistic" title="Champion statistic">stat</a> that most closely resembles the concept of a 'hitbox', and is the radius used for <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Edge range"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Range" title="Range"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_model.png/20px-Range_model.png?9f7ec" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_model.png/40px-Range_model.png?9f7ec 2x" data-file-width="480" data-file-height="480" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Range" title="Range">edge range</a></span> effects, which include <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Basic attack"><a href="/en-us/Basic_attack" title="Basic attack">basic attacks</a></span>, <a href="/en-us/Direction-targeted" class="mw-redirect" title="Direction-targeted">line collision missiles</a>, rectangular AOEs, and others. The gameplay radius determines the reach of both incoming and outgoing effects: for example, enemies are within a unit's <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Range" title="Range"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/15px-Range_icon.png?ae16f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/30px-Range_icon.png?ae16f 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;basic attack range</span> based on the edge of their gameplay radius and vice versa.
</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Selection_radius.png/44px-Selection_radius.png?7345c" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Selection_radius.png?7345c 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Selection radius</span></div>
<p>A unit's <b>selection radius</b> is a <a href="/en-us/Champion_statistic" title="Champion statistic">stat</a> that determines the horizontally furthest point from the center of their model that other players' cursor is allowed to be, while still maintaining the ability to select that unit.
</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Pathing_radius.png/44px-Pathing_radius.png?ee4af" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Pathing_radius.png?ee4af 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Pathing radius</span></div>
<p>A unit's <b>pathing radius</b> is a <a href="/en-us/Champion_statistic" title="Champion statistic">stat</a> that determines the gameplay area they occupy for unit-collision and pathfinding logic. A unit's center cannot intersect with another unit's <b>pathing radius</b>, unless one of them is <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Ghosted"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Unit_collision" title="Unit collision"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ghost.png/20px-Ghost.png?ee615" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Ghost.png/40px-Ghost.png?ee615 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Unit_collision" title="Unit collision">ghosted</a></span>.
</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Selection_height.png/44px-Selection_height.png?8e760" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="43" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Selection_height.png?8e760 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="71" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Selection height</span></div>
A unit's <b>selection height</b> is a <a href="/en-us/Champion_statistic" title="Champion statistic">stat</a> that determines the vertically furthest point from the center of their model at the ground that other players' cursor is allowed to be, while still maintaining the ability to select that unit.<hr style="width:90%; border:solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25); border-width:0px 0px 1px 0px;" />
<p>
Gameplay in <a href="/en-us/League_of_Legends" title="League of Legends">League of Legends</a> takes place in two dimensions no matter the visuals. However, a virtual <i>height</i> dimension that is perpendicular to the ground creates the game's three-dimensional view, which in combination with the camera's perspective necessitates the usage of the <b>selection height</b>.</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Acquisition_range.png/44px-Acquisition_range.png?72c63" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Acquisition_range.png?72c63 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Acquisition radius</span></div>
<p>A unit's <b>acquisition range</b> is a <a href="/en-us/Champion_statistic" title="Champion statistic">stat</a> that determines the distance at which they will acquire <a href="/en-us/Basic_attack" title="Basic attack">attack</a> targets when a target unit is not specified by the player.
</p>
<ul><li>Auto-attacking <i>automatically</i> orders an idle champion to acquire enemies within this range. This can be disabled in the <a href="/en-us/Settings" title="Settings">Settings</a>.</li>
<li>Attack-move commands scan for targets within this range while moving toward a given location.</li></ul>
<p><span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Range" title="Range"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/15px-Range_icon.png?ae16f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/30px-Range_icon.png?ae16f 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<a href="/en-us/Range" title="Range"><span style="color: #AEB3BD; white-space:normal">Attack range</span></a></span> bonuses modify the champion's <b>acquisition range</b> by the same amount.
</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Jungle_icon.png/44px-Jungle_icon.png?9225d" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Jungle_icon.png/88px-Jungle_icon.png?9225d 2x" data-file-width="136" data-file-height="136" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Jungle</span></div>
<p>Within a <a href="/en-us/Drafted_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Drafted team">drafted team</a>, the <i>Jungler</i> is the champion assigned to the jungle. A <i>Jungler</i> needs to be able to <a href="/en-us/Jungling" title="Jungling">clear jungle camps</a> without too much difficulty and ambush other champions in lane.
</p>
<p>
<span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Diver"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Diver" title="Diver"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Fighter_icon.png/20px-Fighter_icon.png?e3f07" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Fighter_icon.png/40px-Fighter_icon.png?e3f07 2x" data-file-width="192" data-file-height="192" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Diver" class="mw-redirect" title="Diver">Divers</a></span>, <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Assassin"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Assassin" title="Assassin"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Slayer_icon.png/20px-Slayer_icon.png?dde86" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Slayer_icon.png/40px-Slayer_icon.png?dde86 2x" data-file-width="192" data-file-height="192" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Assassin" class="mw-redirect" title="Assassin">Assassins</a></span>, <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Skirmisher"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Skirmisher" title="Skirmisher"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Slayer_icon.png/20px-Slayer_icon.png?dde86" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Slayer_icon.png/40px-Slayer_icon.png?dde86 2x" data-file-width="192" data-file-height="192" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Skirmisher" class="mw-redirect" title="Skirmisher">Skirmishers</a></span>, and <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Vanguard"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Champion_classes/Tank#Vanguards" title="Champion classes/Tank"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Tank_icon.png/20px-Tank_icon.png?d2561" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Tank_icon.png/40px-Tank_icon.png?d2561 2x" data-file-width="192" data-file-height="192" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Champion_classes/Tank#Vanguards" title="Champion classes/Tank">Vanguards</a></span> are the most likely champions to be selected in the <i>Jungler</i> position.</p></div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Specialist_icon.png/44px-Specialist_icon.png?a3530" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Specialist_icon.png/88px-Specialist_icon.png?a3530 2x" data-file-width="136" data-file-height="136" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Specialist</span></div>
<p><i>Specialists</i> are champions that do not fit into the "neat little boxes" of the other classes, and represent Riot's ideal of having a champion roster with a lot of distinctiveness and diversity.
</p>
<p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p><dl><dt>Examples</dt></dl>
<ul><li><span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Azir" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Azir" title="An icon representing Azir"><img alt="An icon representing Azir" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Azir_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Azir_OriginalSquare.png?95417" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Azir_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Azir_OriginalSquare.png?95417 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Azir" title="Azir">Azir</a></span></span></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Teemo" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Teemo" title="An icon representing Teemo"><img alt="An icon representing Teemo" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Teemo_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Teemo_OriginalSquare.png?783d6" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Teemo_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Teemo_OriginalSquare.png?783d6 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Teemo" title="Teemo">Teemo</a></span></span></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Heimerdinger" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Heimerdinger" title="An icon representing Heimerdinger"><img alt="An icon representing Heimerdinger" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Heimerdinger_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Heimerdinger_OriginalSquare.png?80a6b" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Heimerdinger_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Heimerdinger_OriginalSquare.png?80a6b 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Heimerdinger" title="Heimerdinger">Heimerdinger</a></span></span></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Singed" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Singed" title="An icon representing Singed"><img alt="An icon representing Singed" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Singed_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Singed_OriginalSquare.png?e9e6e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Singed_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Singed_OriginalSquare.png?e9e6e 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Singed" title="Singed">Singed</a></span></span></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Gangplank" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Gangplank" title="An icon representing Gangplank"><img alt="An icon representing Gangplank" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Gangplank_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Gangplank_OriginalSquare.png?6b5cf" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Gangplank_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Gangplank_OriginalSquare.png?6b5cf 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Gangplank" title="Gangplank">Gangplank</a></span></span><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p></li></ul></div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Slayer_icon.png/44px-Slayer_icon.png?dde86" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Slayer_icon.png/88px-Slayer_icon.png?dde86 2x" data-file-width="192" data-file-height="192" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Assassin (Legacy)</span></div>
<b>Assassins</b> are fragile but agile damage-focused melee champions that look to swiftly take down their targets.

</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Mage_icon.png/44px-Mage_icon.png?c4c84" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Mage_icon.png/88px-Mage_icon.png?c4c84 2x" data-file-width="192" data-file-height="192" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Mage (Legacy)</span></div>
<p><b>Mages</b> are offensive casters that seek to cripple and burn down the opposition through their potent spells.
</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Mana_resource.png/44px-Mana_resource.png?5be85" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Mana_resource.png/88px-Mana_resource.png?5be85 2x" data-file-width="168" data-file-height="168" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Mana</span></div>
<p><span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Mana" title="Mana"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Mana_icon.png/15px-Mana_icon.png?9fefd" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Mana_icon.png/30px-Mana_icon.png?9fefd 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<b>Mana</b></span> (also known as <b>MP</b>) is a <a href="/en-us/Champion_statistic" title="Champion statistic">stat</a> that is the resource of many <a href="/en-us/Champion" title="Champion">champions</a> necessary to cast most of their <a href="/en-us/Champion_ability" title="Champion ability">abilities</a>. Mana can be restored via <a href="/en-us/Mana_regeneration" title="Mana regeneration">mana regeneration</a> and some <a href="/en-us/Champion_ability" title="Champion ability">abilities</a>, <a href="/en-us/Item" title="Item">items</a>, <a href="/en-us/Rune" title="Rune">runes</a>, and <a href="/en-us/Buff" title="Buff">buffs</a>.<br /><br /><b>Mana</b> is represented in-game by the blue bar within the HUD, indicating the champion's <b>current</b> mana and <b>maximum</b> mana. <b>Current</b> mana is reduced by expenditure through paying an ability's mana <i>cost</i>.
</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ranged_role.png/44px-Ranged_role.png?62375" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Ranged_role.png/88px-Ranged_role.png?62375 2x" data-file-width="168" data-file-height="168" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Ranged</span></div>
<p><b>Ranged</b> champions have a basic attack <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Range" title="Range"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/15px-Range_icon.png?ae16f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/30px-Range_icon.png?ae16f 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;range</span> usually beyond 300 units. Many deal damage through projectiles, which are subject to mitigating effects like <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Yasuo" data-ability="Wind Wall" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Yasuo#Wind_Wall" title="An icon for Yasuo&#39;s ability Wind Wall"><img alt="An icon for Yasuo&#39;s ability Wind Wall" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Yasuo_Wind_Wall.png/20px-Yasuo_Wind_Wall.png?0ffbb" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Yasuo_Wind_Wall.png/40px-Yasuo_Wind_Wall.png?0ffbb 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Yasuo#Wind_Wall" title="Yasuo">Wind Wall</a></span></span>. Some champions can shift between a ranged and melee form, and certain items/runes differ for ranged characters.
</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ivern_Brushmaker.png/44px-Ivern_Brushmaker.png?4c89b" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Ivern_Brushmaker.png?4c89b 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Brush</span></div>
<p><b>Brush</b> is a common terrain feature that obstructs <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Sight"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Sight" title="Sight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Sight_icon.png/20px-Sight_icon.png?0aaf0" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Sight_icon.png?0aaf0 2x" data-file-width="26" data-file-height="26" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Sight" title="Sight">sight</a></span> for any unit outside of it.
</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ghost.png/44px-Ghost.png?ee615" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Ghost.png?ee615 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Ghosted</span></div>
<p>A unit that is <b>ghosted</b> ignores <a href="/en-us/Unit_collision" title="Unit collision">unit collision</a>, allowing them to move through other units and other units to move through them.
</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Champion_icon.png/44px-Champion_icon.png?2d7b0" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Champion_icon.png/88px-Champion_icon.png?2d7b0 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Champion</span></div>
<p><b>Champions</b> are the player-controlled characters in <a href="/en-us/League_of_Legends" title="League of Legends">League of Legends</a>. Each champion possesses unique abilities and <a href="/en-us/Champion_attributes" class="mw-redirect" title="Champion attributes">attributes</a>.
</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/Monster_icon.png?e9efe" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="24" data-file-height="24" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Monster</span></div>
<p><b>Monsters</b> are neutral units in <b>League of Legends</b>. Unlike <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Minions"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Minion" title="Minion"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Minion_icon.png/20px-Minion_icon.png?b3697" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Minion_icon.png/40px-Minion_icon.png?b3697 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Minion" title="Minion">minions</a></span>, monsters do not fight for either team, and will only do so if <i>aggroed</i> (provoked) – with the exception of the <span class="inline-image unit-icon label-after" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param=""><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Rift_Scuttler" title="An icon representing Rift Scuttler"><img alt="An icon representing Rift Scuttler" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Rift_ScuttlerSquare.png/20px-Rift_ScuttlerSquare.png?c9a70" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Rift_ScuttlerSquare.png/40px-Rift_ScuttlerSquare.png?c9a70 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Rift_Scuttler" class="mw-redirect" title="Rift Scuttler">Rift Scuttler</a></span></span>, which simply runs away when attacked.
</p>

It does not bypass <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Nearsight"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nearsight" title="Nearsight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nearsight_icon.png/20px-Nearsight_icon.png?70ec5" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nearsight_icon.png/40px-Nearsight_icon.png?70ec5 2x" data-file-width="65" data-file-height="65" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Nearsight" class="mw-redirect" title="Nearsight">nearsight</a></span> effects.
</p>

white-space:normal">magic damage</span> to nearby enemies upon arrival.</td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top; padding: 0.5em; text-align: left;"><span class="template_sbc"><b><i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Prowl" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Prowl" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Prowl" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/20px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Prowl.png/40px-Nidalee_Prowl.png?6998a 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Prowl">Hunted</a></span></span></i> Bonus:</b></span> <i>Pounce</i> has increased range when cast near <i>Hunted</i> targets.</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ghost.png/44px-Ghost.png?ee615" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Ghost.png?ee615 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Ghosted</span></div>
<p>A unit that is <b>ghosted</b> ignores <a href="/en-us/Unit_collision" title="Unit collision">unit collision</a>, allowing them to move through other units and other units to move through them.
</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/Sight_icon.png?0aaf0" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="26" data-file-height="26" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Sight</span></div>
<b>Sight</b> is a property of <a href="/en-us/Unit" class="mw-disambig" title="Unit">units</a>, <a href="/en-us/Structures" class="mw-redirect" title="Structures">structures</a>, certain <a href="/en-us/Summoner_spell" title="Summoner spell">summoner spells</a>, <a href="/en-us/Item" title="Item">items</a>, and <a href="/en-us/Champion_ability" title="Champion ability">abilities</a> that represents a team possessing vision of a target area or unit. It is always <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Center range"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Range" title="Range"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_center.png/20px-Range_center.png?cbed4" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_center.png/40px-Range_center.png?cbed4 2x" data-file-width="480" data-file-height="480" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Range" title="Range">center range</a></span>. A line of vision cannot extend beyond terrain or an unrevealed brush.<hr style="width:90%; border:solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25); border-width:0px 0px 1px 0px;" />
<p>
<b>Sight</b> can also refer to an effect that makes a unit visible regardless of the fog of war or <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Brush"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Brush" title="Brush"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ivern_Brushmaker.png/20px-Ivern_Brushmaker.png?4c89b" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Ivern_Brushmaker.png/40px-Ivern_Brushmaker.png?4c89b 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Brush" title="Brush">brush</a></span>, allowing them to be targeted. <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Standard sight"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Sight#Standard_sight" title="Sight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Reveal_icon.png/20px-Reveal_icon.png?8f092" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Reveal_icon.png/40px-Reveal_icon.png?8f092 2x" data-file-width="256" data-file-height="256" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Sight#Standard_sight" title="Sight">Standard sight</a></span> cannot see <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Stealth"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Stealth" title="Stealth"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Teemo_Guerrilla_Warfare.png/20px-Teemo_Guerrilla_Warfare.png?116ff" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Teemo_Guerrilla_Warfare.png/40px-Teemo_Guerrilla_Warfare.png?116ff 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Stealth" title="Stealth">stealthed</a></span> units, but <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="True sight"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Sight#True_sight" title="Sight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/True_Sight_icon.png/20px-True_Sight_icon.png?8830f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/True_Sight_icon.png/40px-True_Sight_icon.png?8830f 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Sight#True_sight" title="Sight">True Sight</a></span> can.
</p><ul><li><span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Nearsight"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nearsight" title="Nearsight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nearsight_icon.png/20px-Nearsight_icon.png?70ec5" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nearsight_icon.png/40px-Nearsight_icon.png?70ec5 2x" data-file-width="65" data-file-height="65" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Nearsight" class="mw-redirect" title="Nearsight">Nearsight</a></span> is a <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Crowd control"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Crowd_control" title="Crowd control"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Stun_icon.png/20px-Stun_icon.png?cacf8" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Stun_icon.png/40px-Stun_icon.png?cacf8 2x" data-file-width="65" data-file-height="65" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Crowd_control" title="Crowd control">crowd control</a></span> debuff that inhibits <b>sight</b>; allied vision is lost in addition to a reduced sight radius.</li>
<li><span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Obscured vision"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Sight#Obscured_vision" title="Sight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Sweeper_Drone_icon.png/20px-Sweeper_Drone_icon.png?6e3eb" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Sweeper_Drone_icon.png/40px-Sweeper_Drone_icon.png?6e3eb 2x" data-file-width="80" data-file-height="80" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Sight#Obscured_vision" title="Sight">Obscured vision</a></span> is similar to <b>sight</b> in a way that it can observe units, but does not render units <i>targetable</i>, rather it exposes their position and informs of their presence.</li>
<li><span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Unobstructed vision"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Sight#Unobstructed_vision" title="Sight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Stealth_Ward_icon.png/20px-Stealth_Ward_icon.png?0305b" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Stealth_Ward_icon.png/40px-Stealth_Ward_icon.png?0305b 2x" data-file-width="80" data-file-height="80" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Sight#Unobstructed_vision" title="Sight">Unobstructed vision</a></span> is a form of <b>sight</b> that allows a unit to be able to see their full vision radius, ignoring any obstructions that would otherwise restrict visibility.</li>
<li>All effects that use <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Unit-targeted"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Unit-targeted" title="Unit-targeted"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Jax_Leap_Strike.png/20px-Jax_Leap_Strike.png?0e517" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Jax_Leap_Strike.png/40px-Jax_Leap_Strike.png?0e517 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Unit-targeted" class="mw-redirect" title="Unit-targeted">unit-targeting</a></span> require <b>sight</b> of the target. Delayed <i>unit-targeted</i> attacks and spells can cancel if <b>sight</b> of the selected target is suddenly lost.<p class="mw-empty-elt"></p></li></ul>

</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Arena_icon.png/44px-Arena_icon.png?c4c60" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Arena_icon.png/88px-Arena_icon.png?c4c60 2x" data-file-width="210" data-file-height="210" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Arena</span></div>
<figure class="mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/File:Arena_Promo_03.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Arena_Promo_03.jpg/250px-Arena_Promo_03.jpg?b6d6e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="129" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Arena_Promo_03.jpg/500px-Arena_Promo_03.jpg?b6d6e 2x" data-file-width="4800" data-file-height="2480" /></a><figcaption></figcaption></figure> <b>Arena</b> is a team deathmatch game mode organized in a tournament format that consists of eight teams of two players fighting on six different battlefields. Teams brawl in rotating combat rounds while powering themselves up with unique Augments and Items and using multiple environmental features to their advantage, in a display of both deeply tactical and highly explosive combat until the last team standing.
<dl><dt>Regular Modes</dt></dl>
<ul><li><i>8-Team Round-Robin Tournament</i></li></ul>
<dl><dt>Battlefields — The Grand Reckoning</dt>
<dd></dd></dl>
<ul><li><i>Ancestral Woods</i></li>
<li><i>Desert Oasis</i></li>
<li><i>Frostbite Thicket</i></li>
<li><i>Koi Pond</i></li>
<li><i>Magma Chamber</i></li>
<li><i>Reckoner Arena</i></li></ul>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_center.png/44px-Range_center.png?cbed4" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_center.png/88px-Range_center.png?cbed4 2x" data-file-width="480" data-file-height="480" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Centered range</span></div>
<p><b>Centered range</b> is calculated from the <b>center</b> of a source unit's hitbox to the <b>center</b> of a target unit's hitbox.
</p>
<ul><li>Centered range is used for most <a href="/en-us/Targeting#Unit-targeted" title="Targeting">unit-targeted</a> abilities.</li>
<li>It is <i>less</i> effective and may seem to have diminished reach against <a href="/en-us/Unit_size" title="Unit size">large</a> units.</li></ul>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_model.png/44px-Range_model.png?9f7ec" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_model.png/88px-Range_model.png?9f7ec 2x" data-file-width="480" data-file-height="480" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Edge range</span></div>
<p><b>Edge range</b> is calculated from the <b>edge</b> of a source unit's hitbox to the <b>edge</b> of a target unit's hitbox.
</p>
<ul><li>Edge range is mostly used for <a href="/en-us/Basic_attack" title="Basic attack">basic attacks</a>; <a href="/en-us/Targeting#Direction-targeted" title="Targeting">skill shots</a>; and point-blank areas of effect (including <a href="/en-us/Aura" title="Aura">auras</a>).</li>
<li>These become <i>more</i> effective against large champions, as the source gains more reach against them. This may be favorable or unfavorable: durable champions tend to be larger and thus easier to hit, and frail champions tend to be smaller and more difficult to hit.</li></ul>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Annie_Disintegrate.png/44px-Annie_Disintegrate.png?bbde6" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Annie_Disintegrate.png?bbde6 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Spell damage</span></div>
<i>Spell damage</i> is the damage type dealt by most single target abilities, as well as a select few basic attacks, items and runes. <i>Spell damage</i> is not exclusive to being applied by purely <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Physical damage"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Physical_damage" title="Physical damage"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Attack_damage.png/20px-Attack_damage.png?26459" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Attack_damage.png/40px-Attack_damage.png?26459 2x" data-file-width="163" data-file-height="163" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Physical_damage" title="Physical damage">physical</a></span>, <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Magic damage"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Magic_damage" title="Magic damage"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Magic_damage.png/20px-Magic_damage.png?2db19" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Magic_damage.png/40px-Magic_damage.png?2db19 2x" data-file-width="163" data-file-height="163" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Magic_damage" title="Magic damage">magic</a></span> or <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="True damage"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/True_damage" title="True damage"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Hybrid_penetration.png/20px-Hybrid_penetration.png?d6752" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Hybrid_penetration.png/40px-Hybrid_penetration.png?d6752 2x" data-file-width="163" data-file-height="163" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/True_damage" title="True damage">true damage</a></span>, and instead can be dealt by any of the three damage sub-types.<hr style="width:90%; border:solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25); border-width:0px 0px 1px 0px;" />
<p>
Many effects are triggered whenever you deal an instance of <i>spell damage</i>. For example:
</p><ul><li><span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Rylai&#39;s Crystal Scepter" data-game="lol"><span Scepter</a></span></span>, <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Liandry&#39;s Torment" data-game="lol"><span <p>
Effects triggered by damage sub-types will occur (e.g. <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Black Cleaver" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Black_Cleaver" title="An icon for the item Black Cleaver"><img alt="An icon for the item Black Cleaver" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Black_Cleaver_item.png/20px-Black_Cleaver_item.png?98eed" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Black_Cleaver_item.png/40px-Black_Cleaver_item.png?98eed 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Black_Cleaver" title="Black Cleaver">Black Cleaver</a></span></span> on instances of <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; <p><b>Swiftplay</b> is <a href="/en-us/Normal_game" title="Normal game">Normal game</a> queue for 5v5 <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Classic"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Classic" title="Classic"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Red_Nexus_icon.png/20px-Red_Nexus_icon.png?2515b" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Red_Nexus_icon.png?2515b 2x" data-file-width="36" data-file-height="36" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Classic" title="Classic">Classic</a></span> <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Summoner&#39;s rift"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Summoner%27s_Rift" title="Summoner&#39;s Rift"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Summoner%27s_Rift_icon.png/20px-Summoner%27s_Rift_icon.png?7a043" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Summoner%27s_Rift_icon.png/40px-Summoner%27s_Rift_icon.png?7a043 2x" data-file-width="100" data-file-height="100" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Summoner%27s_Rift" title="Summoner&#39;s Rift">Summoner's Rift</a></span>.
</p>
Players skip <a href="/en-us/Champion_select" class="mw-redirect" title="Champion select">champion select</a> by picking their champions beforehand in the lobby, then enter a game that has accelerated game rules (resulting in faster games overall)—such as gaining extra <span class="inline-image label-after" style="display:inline;color:#E2BA3D;white-space:pre;text-shadow:-1px 0 black,0 1px black,1px 0 black,0 -1px black;" data-param=""><span style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Gold" title="An icon representing Gold"><img alt="An icon representing Gold" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Gold_colored_icon.png/20px-Gold_colored_icon.png?39991" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Gold_colored_icon.png/40px-Gold_colored_icon.png?39991 2x" data-file-width="96" data-file-height="96" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;">gold</span></span> from nearby <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Minion"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Minion" title="Minion"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Minion_icon.png/20px-Minion_icon.png?b3697" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Minion_icon.png/40px-Minion_icon.png?b3697 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Minion" title="Minion">minion</a></span> deaths, <span class="inline-image unit-icon label-after" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param=""><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Rift_Herald" title="An icon representing Rift Herald"><img alt="An icon representing Rift Herald" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Rift_HeraldSquare.png/20px-Rift_HeraldSquare.png?0bb4f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Rift_HeraldSquare.png/40px-Rift_HeraldSquare.png?0bb4f 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Rift_Herald" title="Rift Herald">Rift Herald</a></span></span> and <span class="inline-image unit-icon label-after" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param=""><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Baron_Nashor" title="An icon representing Baron Nashor"><img alt="An icon representing Baron Nashor" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Baron_NashorSquare.png/20px-Baron_NashorSquare.png?05e38" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Baron_NashorSquare.png/40px-Baron_NashorSquare.png?05e38 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Baron_Nashor" title="Baron Nashor">Baron Nashor</a></span></span> spawning earlier, faster item completion, and more!<hr style="width:90%; border:solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25); border-width:0px 0px 1px 0px;" />
<p>
<i><b>Swiftplay</b> is currently being tested in the following <a href="/en-us/Server" class="mw-redirect" title="Server">regions</a>: NA, LAN, LAS, EUW, EUNE, RU, BR, TR, TW, VN.</i></p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png/44px-Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png?9f6f9" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Teemo_Noxious_Trap.png?9f6f9 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Stealthed trap</span></div>
<p><b>Stealthed traps</b> are <a href="/en-us/Champion_summoned_units" title="Champion summoned units">units</a> that enter <i>stealth</i> shortly after being summoned, last for a duration, and are <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Untargetable"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Untargetable" title="Untargetable"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Untargetable_icon.png/20px-Untargetable_icon.png?c022c" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Untargetable_icon.png/40px-Untargetable_icon.png?c022c 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Untargetable" class="mw-redirect" title="Untargetable">untargetable</a></span> until they are <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="True sight"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Sight#True_sight" title="Sight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/True_Sight_icon.png/20px-True_Sight_icon.png?8830f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/True_Sight_icon.png/40px-True_Sight_icon.png?8830f 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Sight#True_sight" title="Sight">revealed</a></span>. They may be revealed and made targetable once again by <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Control Ward" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Control_Ward" title="An icon for the item Control Ward"><img alt="An icon for the item Control Ward" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Control_Ward_item.png/20px-Control_Ward_item.png?dae36" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Control_Ward_item.png/40px-Control_Ward_item.png?dae36 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Control_Ward" title="Control Ward">Control Wards</a></span></span>, <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Sweeper drone"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Oracle_Lens" title="Oracle Lens"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Sweeper_Drone_icon.png/20px-Sweeper_Drone_icon.png?6e3eb" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Sweeper_Drone_icon.png/40px-Sweeper_Drone_icon.png?6e3eb 2x" data-file-width="80" data-file-height="80" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Oracle_Lens" title="Oracle Lens">Sweeper Drones</a></span> (e.g. from <span class="champion-ability-icon"><span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Fiddlesticks" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Fiddlesticks" title="An icon representing Fiddlesticks"><img alt="An icon representing Fiddlesticks" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Fiddlesticks_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Fiddlesticks_OriginalSquare.png?1082b" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Fiddlesticks_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Fiddlesticks_OriginalSquare.png?1082b 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Fiddlesticks" title="Fiddlesticks">Fiddlesticks'</a></span></span> <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Fiddlesticks" data-ability="A Harmless Scarecrow" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Fiddlesticks#A_Harmless_Scarecrow" title="An icon for Fiddlesticks&#39;s item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Oracle Lens" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Oracle_Lens" title="An icon for the item Oracle Lens"><img alt="An icon for the item Oracle Lens"
