</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Melee_role.png/44px-Melee_role.png?166b1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Melee_role.png/88px-Melee_role.png?166b1 2x" data-file-width="168" data-file-height="168" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Melee</span></div>
<p><b>Melee</b> champions have a basic attack <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Range" title="Range"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/15px-Range_icon.png?ae16f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Range_icon.png/30px-Range_icon.png?ae16f 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;range</span> usually within 200 units. A melee attack does not use a projectile to deal damage, therefore not subject to effects that mitigate projectiles, like <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Yasuo" data-ability="Wind Wall" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Yasuo#Wind_Wall" title="An icon for Yasuo&#39;s ability Wind Wall"><img alt="An icon for Yasuo&#39;s ability Wind Wall" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Yasuo_Wind_Wall.png/20px-Yasuo_Wind_Wall.png?0ffbb" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Yasuo_Wind_Wall.png/40px-Yasuo_Wind_Wall.png?0ffbb 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Yasuo#Wind_Wall" title="Yasuo">Wind Wall</a></span></span>. Some champions can shift between a ranged and melee form, and certain items/runes differ for melee characters.
</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Brand_Blaze.png/44px-Brand_Blaze.png?c8036" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Brand_Blaze.png?c8036 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Persistent damage</span></div>
<i>Persistent damage</i> is the damage type dealt primarily by damage over time (DoT) abilities. Most sources of <i>persistent damage</i> have the <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Magic damage"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Magic_damage" title="Magic damage"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Magic_damage.png/20px-Magic_damage.png?2db19" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Magic_damage.png/40px-Magic_damage.png?2db19 2x" data-file-width="163" data-file-height="163" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Magic_damage" title="Magic damage">magic damage</a></span> sub-type, but this is not guaranteed.<hr style="width:90%; border:solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25); border-width:0px 0px 1px 0px;" />
<p>
Many effects are triggered whenever you deal an instance of <i>persistent damage</i>. For example:
</p><ul><li><span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Rylai&#39;s Crystal Scepter" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Rylai%27s_Crystal_Scepter" title="An icon for the item Scepter</a></span></span>, <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Liandry&#39;s Torment" data-game="lol"><span <li><span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Omnivamp"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Vamp#Omnivamp" title="Vamp"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Omnivamp_colored_icon.png/20px-Omnivamp_colored_icon.png?2d097" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Omnivamp_colored_icon.png/40px-Omnivamp_colored_icon.png?2d097 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Vamp#Omnivamp" title="Vamp">Omnivamp</a></span> and <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Physical vamp"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Vamp#Physical_vamp" title="Vamp"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Life_steal_icon.png/20px-Life_steal_icon.png?e8287" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Life_steal_icon.png/40px-Life_steal_icon.png?e8287 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Vamp#Physical_vamp" title="Vamp">Physical vamp</a></span> (where applicable) heal for a percentage of damage dealt.</li>

<p>
Effects triggered by damage sub-types will occur (e.g. <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="The Black Cleaver" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/The_Black_Cleaver" title="An icon for the item The Black Cleaver"><img alt="An icon for the item The Black Cleaver" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Black_Cleaver_item.png/20px-Black_Cleaver_item.png?98eed" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Black_Cleaver_item.png/40px-Black_Cleaver_item.png?98eed 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/The_Black_Cleaver" class="mw-redirect" title="The Black Cleaver">The Black Cleaver</a></span></span> on instances of <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Physical damage"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Physical_damage" title="Physical damage"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Attack_damage.png/20px-Attack_damage.png?26459" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Attack_damage.png/40px-Attack_damage.png?26459 2x" data-file-width="163" data-file-height="163" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Physical_damage" title="Physical damage">Physical damage</a></span> and <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Morellonomicon" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Morellonomicon" title="An icon for the item Morellonomicon"><img alt="An icon for the item Morellonomicon" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Morellonomicon_item.png/20px-Morellonomicon_item.png?e9bc2" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Morellonomicon_item.png/40px-Morellonomicon_item.png?e9bc2 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Morellonomicon" title="Morellonomicon">Morellonomicon</a></span></span> on instances of <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; font-weight: bold;">Heal</span></div>
<b>Healing</b> replenishes a unit's <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Health" title="Health"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Health_icon.png/15px-Health_icon.png?f8c57" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Health_icon.png/30px-Health_icon.png?f8c57 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<span style="color: #21B053; white-space:normal"><b>current</b> health</span></span>, but never above their <span style="color: #21B053; white-space:normal"><b>maximum</b> health</span>.<hr style="width:90%; border:solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25); border-width:0px 0px 1px 0px;" />
<p>
Outgoing heals can trigger bonus effects from <span class="inline-image label-after rune-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-rune="Summon Aery" data-game="lol"><span srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Summon_Aery_rune.png/40px-Summon_Aery_rune.png?aab8d 2x" data-file-width="256" data-file-height="256" /></a></span></span> <span style="word-break: keep-all;"><a href="/en-us/Summon_Aery" title="Summon Aery">Summon Aery</a></span></span>, <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Ardent Censer" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Ghosted"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Unit_collision" title="Unit collision"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ghost.png/20px-Ghost.png?ee615" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Ghost.png/40px-Ghost.png?ee615 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Unit_collision" title="Unit collision">ghosted</a></span> and gains <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Movement_speed" title="Movement speed"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Movement_speed_icon.png/15px-Movement_speed_icon.png?f928e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Movement_speed_icon.png/30px-Movement_speed_icon.png?f928e 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<span style="color: #9FFF4D; white-space:normal"><b>bonus</b> movement speed</span></span> for a short time, increased when facing a nearby enemy <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Champion"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Champion" title="Champion"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Champion_icon.png/20px-Champion_icon.png?2d7b0" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Champion_icon.png/40px-Champion_icon.png?2d7b0 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Champion" title="Champion">champion</a></span>. These bonuses briefly persist after exiting brush.</td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top; padding: 0.5em; text-align: left;"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Innate - Hunt:</b></span> Hitting nearby <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Monsters"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Monster" title="Monster"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Monster_icon.png/20px-Monster_icon.png?e9efe" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Monster_icon.png?e9efe 2x" data-file-width="24" data-file-height="24" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Monster" title="Monster">monsters</a></span> or enemy champions with <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Javelin Toss" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Javelin_Toss" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Javelin Toss"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Javelin Toss" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png/20px-Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png?9d69e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png/40px-Nidalee_Javelin_Toss.png?9d69e 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Javelin_Toss">Javelin Toss</a></span></span></i> or <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Bushwhack" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Bushwhack" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Bushwhack"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Bushwhack" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Bushwhack.png/20px-Nidalee_Bushwhack.png?2263d" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Bushwhack.png/40px-Nidalee_Bushwhack.png?2263d 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Bushwhack">Bushwhack</a></span></span></i> will apply a <i>Hunted</i> mark and <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="True sight"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Sight#True_sight" title="Sight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/True_Sight_icon.png/20px-True_Sight_icon.png?8830f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/True_Sight_icon.png/40px-True_Sight_icon.png?8830f 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Sight#True_sight" title="Sight">reveal</a></span> them for a few seconds. During this time, <b>Nidalee</b> gains <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Movement_speed" title="Movement speed"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Movement_speed_icon.png/15px-Movement_speed_icon.png?f928e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Movement_speed_icon.png/30px-Movement_speed_icon.png?f928e 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<span style="color: #9FFF4D; white-space:normal"><b>bonus</b> movement speed</span></span>, increased when facing a <i>Hunted</i> target.</td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top; padding: 0.5em; text-align: left;"><b>Nidalee's</b> first use of <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Takedown" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Takedown" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Takedown" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/20px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Takedown.png/40px-Nidalee_Takedown.png?11a28 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Takedown">Takedown</a></span></span></i> and <i><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Nidalee" data-ability="Pounce" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Nidalee#Pounce" title="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Pounce"><img alt="An icon for Nidalee&#39;s ability Pounce" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Pounce.png/20px-Nidalee_Pounce.png?b56c7" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Nidalee_Pounce.png/40px-Nidalee_Pounce.png?b56c7 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Pounce">Pounce</a></span></span></i> against <i>Hunted</i> targets are empowered.</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Vi_Relentless_Force_2.png/44px-Vi_Relentless_Force_2.png?9f7e9" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Vi_Relentless_Force_2.png?9f7e9 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Uncancellable windup</span></div>
Some effects cause a basic attack to have an <b>uncancellable windup</b>. Unlike normal basic attacks and similar to the cast time of a spell, the windup of these attacks cannot be <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Interrupt"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Crowd_control#Disruption" title="Crowd control"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Silence_icon.png/20px-Silence_icon.png?70ec5" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Silence_icon.png/40px-Silence_icon.png?70ec5 2x" data-file-width="65" data-file-height="65" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Crowd_control#Disruption" title="Crowd control">interrupted</a></span> by neither the user themselves nor any status effect, other than <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Death"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Death" title="Death"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Death.png/20px-Death.png?be9bc" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Death.png/40px-Death.png?be9bc 2x" data-file-width="52" data-file-height="52" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Death" title="Death">death</a></span>, <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Polymorph"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Types_of_Crowd_Control#Polymorph" title="Types of Crowd Control"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Silence_icon.png/20px-Silence_icon.png?70ec5" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Silence_icon.png/40px-Silence_icon.png?70ec5 2x" data-file-width="65" data-file-height="65" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Types_of_Crowd_Control#Polymorph" title="Types of Crowd Control">polymorph</a></span> and <span class="champion-ability-icon"><span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Quinn" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Quinn" title="An icon representing Quinn"><img alt="An icon representing Quinn" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Quinn_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Quinn_OriginalSquare.png?098bd" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Quinn_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Quinn_OriginalSquare.png?098bd 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Quinn" title="Quinn">Quinn's</a></span></span> <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Quinn" data-ability="Vault" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Quinn#Vault" title="An icon for Quinn&#39;s ability Vault"><img alt="An icon for Quinn&#39;s ability Vault" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Quinn_Vault.png/20px-Quinn_Vault.png?eefca" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Quinn_Vault.png/40px-Quinn_Vault.png?eefca 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Quinn#Vault" title="Quinn">Vault</a></span></span></span>, and sometimes <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Untargetability"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Untargetable" title="Untargetable"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Untargetable_icon.png/20px-Untargetable_icon.png?c022c" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Untargetable_icon.png/40px-Untargetable_icon.png?c022c 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Untargetable" class="mw-redirect" title="Untargetable">untargetability</a></span> and range.<hr style="width:90%; border:solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25); border-width:0px 0px 1px 0px;" />
<p>
Any effect that would disrupt an attack's windup, aside from the ones noted above, are ignored by basic attacks with <b>uncancellable windups</b>. If the attack doesn't lock out other abilities, they may be used normally, and the basic attack will hit during the ability cast.</p>
</div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Critical_strike_icon.png/44px-Critical_strike_icon.png?d199f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Critical_strike_icon.png/88px-Critical_strike_icon.png?d199f 2x" data-file-width="144" data-file-height="144" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Critical strike</span></div>
<b>Critical strike</b> refers to an effect that deals increased damage under specific circumstances, denoted as <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Critical_strike" title="Critical strike"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Critical_strike_damage_icon.png/15px-Critical_strike_damage_icon.png?4899a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Critical_strike_damage_icon.png/30px-Critical_strike_damage_icon.png?4899a 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;</span> <span style="color: #B4814C; white-space:normal">critical strike damage</span>. The most common form of critical strike occurs on <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Basic attack"><a href="/en-us/Basic_attack" title="Basic attack">basic attacks</a></span>, which triggers based on <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Critical_strike" title="Critical strike"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Critical_strike_chance_icon.png/15px-Critical_strike_chance_icon.png?4899a" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Critical_strike_chance_icon.png/30px-Critical_strike_chance_icon.png?4899a 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<span style="color:orangered; white-space:normal">critical strike chance</span></span>.<hr style="width:90%; border:solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25); border-width:0px 0px 1px 0px;" />
<p>
By default, a critical strike deals 175% of the normal damage. Critical damage modifiers such as <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Infinity Edge" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Infinity_Edge" title="An icon for the item Infinity Edge"><img alt="An icon for the item Infinity Edge" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Infinity_Edge_item.png/20px-Infinity_Edge_item.png?71b4c" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Infinity_Edge_item.png/40px-Infinity_Edge_item.png?71b4c 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Infinity_Edge" title="Infinity Edge">Infinity Edge</a></span></span> can increase this percentage.</p>
</div></div></div>
